The Almighty informs about the Day of Resurrection, that in it some faces will be blackened and some faces will be whitened. The faces of the people of division and disagreement will be blackened, and the faces of the people of the Sunnah and the community will be whitened. The Almighty says here: {And on the Day of Resurrection you will see those who lied against Allah}, meaning in their claiming a partner and a child for Him, {their faces blackened}, meaning by their lying and their fabrication.

His saying: {Is there not in Hell a resting place for the arrogant?} means: is Hell not sufficient as a prison and a refuge for them, wherein is the abode of disgrace and humiliation, because of their arrogance, their tyranny, and their refusal to submit to the truth.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Abu Ubaydillah, nephew of Ibn Wahb, told us, my uncle told us, Isa ibn Abi Isa al-Khayyat told us, from Amr ibn Shu'ayb, from his father, from his grandfather, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Indeed the arrogant will be gathered on the Day of Resurrection resembling ants in the forms of men. Everything of lowliness will overcome them, until they enter a prison of fire in a valley called Bulas, from the Fire of Fires, and they will be given to drink the pus of the people of the Fire, and from the mud of Khabal (corruption)."

His saying: {And Allah will save those who feared Him by their attainment} means: by what had already been decreed for them of felicity and success with Allah. {No harm shall touch them}, meaning on the Day of Resurrection, {nor shall they grieve}, meaning nor shall the greatest terror grieve them. Rather they will be secure from every terror, removed far from every evil, and hopeful of every good.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ أَنَّهُ تَسْوَدُّ فِيهِ وُجُوهٌ، وَتَبْيَضُّ فِيهِ وُجُوهٌ، تَسْوَدُّ وُجُوهُ أَهْلِ الْفُرْقَةِ وَالِاخْتِلَافِ، وَتَبْيَضُّ وُجُوهُ أَهْلِ السُّنَّةِ وَالْجَمَاعَةِ، قَالَ تَعَالَى هَاهُنَا: ﴿وَيَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ تَرَى الَّذِينَ كَذَبُوا عَلَى اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: فِي دَعْوَاهُمْ لَهُ شَرِيكًا وَوَلَدًا ﴿وُجُوهُهُمْ مُسْوَدَّةٌ﴾ أَيْ: بِكَذِبِهِمْ وَافْتِرَائِهِمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَلَيْسَ فِي جَهَنَّمَ مَثْوًى لِلْمُتَكَبِّرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: أَلَيْسَتْ جَهَنَّمُ كَافِيَةً لَهَا سِجْنًا وَمَوْئِلًا لَهُمْ فِيهَا [دَارُ] الْخِزْيِ وَالْهَوَانِ، بِسَبَبِ تَكَبُّرِهِمْ وَتَجَبُّرِهِمْ وَإِبَائِهِمْ عَنِ الِانْقِيَادِ لِلْحَقِّ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ ابْنُ أَخِي ابْنِ وهب، حَدَّثَنَا عَمِّي، حَدَّثَنَا عِيسَى بْنُ أَبِي عِيسَى الْخَيَّاطُ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ شُعَيْبٍ ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ جَدِّهِ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ الْمُتَكَبِّرِينَ يُحْشَرُونَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ أَشْبَاهَ الذَّرِّ فِي صُوَرِ النَّاسِ، يَعْلُوهُمْ كُلُّ شَيْءٍ مِنَ الصَّغَارِ، حَتَّى يَدْخُلُوا سِجْنًا مِنَ النَّارِ فِي وَادٍ يُقَالُ لَهُ بُولَسُ، مِنْ نَارِ الْأَنْيَارِ، وَيُسْقَوْنَ عُصَارَةَ أَهْلِ النَّارِ، وَمِنْ طِينَةِ الخَبَال" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَيُنَجِّي اللَّهُ الَّذِينَ اتَّقَوْا بِمَفَازَتِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: مِمَّا سَبَقَ لَهُمْ مِنَ السَّعَادَةِ وَالْفَوْزِ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ، ﴿لَا يَمَسُّهُمُ السُّوءُ﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، ﴿وَلا هُمْ يَحْزَنُونَ﴾ أَيْ: وَلَا يَحْزُنُهُمُ الْفَزَعُ الْأَكْبَرُ، بَلْ هُمْ آمَنُونَ مِنْ كُلِّ فَزَع، مُزَحْزَحُونَ عَنْ كُلِّ شَرٍّ، مُؤمَلون كُلَّ خَيْرٍ.

---

## 39:62-66 — verses 62-66 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs that He is the Creator of all things, their Lord, their Sovereign Owner, and the One who disposes of them, and everything is under His management, His overpowering, and His safekeeping.

His saying, {To Him belong the maqalid (keys/treasuries) of the heavens and the earth}: Mujahid said: the maqalid are the keys, in Persian. Qatadah, Ibn Zayd, and Sufyan ibn Uyaynah said likewise.

Al-Suddi said: {To Him belong the maqalid of the heavens and the earth}, meaning: the storehouses of the heavens and the earth.

The meaning according to both views is that the reins of all affairs are in His hand. His is the dominion and His is the praise, and He has power over all things. For this reason He said: {And those who disbelieve in the signs of Allah}, meaning: His proofs and evidences, {they are the losers}.

Ibn Abi Hatim reported here a hadith that is very gharib (singular), and there is question regarding its soundness, but we mention it as he mentioned it. He said:

[chain] Yazid ibn Sinan al-Basri narrated to us in Egypt, who said: Yahya ibn Hammad narrated to us, who said: al-Aghlab ibn Tamim narrated to us, from Mukhallad ibn Hudhayl al-Abdi, from Abd al-Rahman al-Madani, from Abdullah ibn Umar, from Uthman ibn Affan, may Allah be pleased with him, that he asked the Messenger of Allah ﷺ about the meaning of {To Him belong the maqalid of the heavens and the earth}. He said: "No one has asked me about it before you, O Uthman." He said: "Its meaning is: there is no god but Allah, and Allah is greatest, and glory be to Allah and praise be to Him, I seek Allah's forgiveness, and there is no power except through Allah, the First and the Last, the Manifest and the Hidden, in His hand is all good, He gives life and causes death, and He has power over all things. Whoever says this, O Uthman, ten times when he rises in the morning will be given six qualities: the first, he will be guarded from Iblis and his troops; the second, he will be given a qintar (a great measure) of reward; the third, a rank will be raised for him in Paradise; the fourth, he will be married to the wide-eyed maidens of Paradise; the fifth, twelve angels will attend him; the sixth, he will be given a reward like one who has recited the Qur'an, the Torah, the Gospel, and the Psalms. And besides this, O Uthman, he will have a reward like one who performed the Hajj and whose Hajj was accepted, and who performed the Umrah and whose Umrah was accepted. And if he dies that day, he will be sealed with the seal of the martyrs."

Abu Ya'la al-Mawsili also related it through the hadith of Yahya ibn Hammad, in the same manner. It is gharib, and there is severe nakarah (objectionable strangeness) in it. And Allah knows best.

His saying, {Say: Is it then other than Allah that you command me to worship, O you ignorant ones?}: They mentioned regarding the reason for its revelation what Ibn Abi Hatim and others reported from Ibn Abbas, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The polytheists, in their ignorance, called the Messenger of Allah ﷺ to the worship of their gods, that they might worship his God together with them. So it was revealed: {Say: Is it then other than Allah that you command me to worship, O you ignorant ones? And it has already been revealed to you and to those before you: if you associate partners with Allah, your deeds will surely come to nothing, and you will surely be among the losers}.

This is like His saying: {And if they had associated partners with Allah, all that they used to do would have come to nothing for them} [al-An'am: 88].

His saying, {Rather, worship Allah alone, and be among the thankful}, meaning: devote worship purely to Allah alone, He has no partner, you and those with you, you and those who follow you and believe you.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ خَالِقُ الْأَشْيَاءِ كُلِّهَا، وَرَبُّهَا وَمَلِيكُهَا وَالْمُتَصَرِّفُ فِيهَا، وَكُلٌّ تَحْتَ تَدْبِيرِهِ وَقَهْرِهِ وكلاءته.

وقوله: ﴿لَهُ مَقَالِيدُ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ ، قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: الْمَقَالِيدُ هِيَ: الْمَفَاتِيحُ بِالْفَارِسِيَّةِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ قَتَادَةُ، وَابْنُ زَيْدٍ، وَسُفْيَانُ ابْنُ عيينة.

وقال السدي: ﴿لَهُ مَقَالِيدُ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ أي: خزائن السموات وَالْأَرْضِ.

وَالْمَعْنَى عَلَى كِلَا الْقَوْلَيْنِ: أَنَّ أزمَّة الْأُمُورِ بِيَدِهِ، لَهُ الْمُلْكُ وَلَهُ الْحَمْدُ، وَهُوَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: حُجَجِهِ وَبَرَاهِينِهِ ﴿أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْخَاسِرُونَ﴾

وَقَدْ رَوَى ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ هَاهُنَا حَدِيثًا غَرِيبًا جِدًّا -وَفِي صِحَّتِهِ نَظَرٌ-وَلَكِنْ نَذْكُرُهُ كَمَا ذَكَرَهُ، فَإِنَّهُ قَالَ:

حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ سِنان الْبَصْرِيُّ بِمِصْرَ، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ حَمَّادٍ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَغْلَبُ بْنُ تَمِيمٍ، عَنْ مُخَلَّدِ بْنِ هُذَيْلٍ الْعَبْدِيِّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ الْمَدَنِيِّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ، عَنْ عُثْمَانَ بْنِ عَفَّانَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّهُ سَأَلَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ عن تفسير: ﴿لَهُ مَقَالِيدُ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ فَقَالَ: "مَا سَأَلَنِي عَنْهَا أَحَدٌ قَبْلَكَ يَا عُثْمَانُ"، قَالَ: "تَفْسِيرُهَا: لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، وَاللَّهُ أَكْبَرُ، وَسُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ وَبِحَمْدِهِ، أَسْتَغْفِرُ اللَّهَ، وَلَا قُوَّةَ إِلَّا بِاللَّهِ، الْأَوَّلِ وَالْآخِرِ، وَالظَّاهِرِ وَالْبَاطِنِ، بِيَدِهِ الْخَيْرُ، يُحْيِي وَيُمِيتُ، وَهُوَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ، مَنْ قَالَهَا يَا عُثْمَانُ إِذَا أَصْبَحَ عَشْرَ مِرَارٍ أُعْطِيَ خِصَالًا سِتًّا: أَمَّا أُولَاهُنَّ: فَيُحْرَسُ مِنْ إِبْلِيسَ وَجُنُودِهِ، وَأَمَّا الثَّانِيَةُ: فَيُعْطَى قِنْطَارًا مِنَ الْأَجْرِ، وَأَمَّا الثَّالِثَةُ: فَتُرْفَعُ لَهُ دَرَجَةٌ فِي الْجَنَّةِ، وَأَمَّا الرَّابِعَةُ: فَيَتَزَوَّجُ مِنَ الْحُورِ الْعِينِ، وَأَمَّا الْخَامِسَةُ: فَيَحْضُرُهُ اثْنَا عَشَرَ مَلَكًا، وَأَمَّا السَّادِسَةُ: فَيُعْطَى مِنَ الْأَجْرِ كَمَنْ قَرَأَ الْقُرْآنَ وَالتَّوْرَاةَ وَالْإِنْجِيلَ وَالزَّبُورَ. وَلَهُ مَعَ هَذَا يَا عُثْمَانُ مِنَ الْأَجْرِ كَمَنْ حَجَّ وَتُقُبِّلَتْ حَجَّتُهُ، وَاعْتَمَرَ فَتُقُبِّلَتْ عُمْرَتُهُ، فَإِنْ مَاتَ مِنْ يَوْمِهِ طُبِعَ بِطَابِعِ الشُّهَدَاءِ".

وَرَوَاهُ أَبُو يَعْلَى الْمُوصِلِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ يَحْيَى بْنِ حَمَّادٍ، بِهِ مِثْلَهُ . وَهُوَ غَرِيبٌ، وَفِيهِ نَكَارَةٌ شَدِيدَةٌ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿قُلْ أَفَغَيْرَ اللَّهِ تَأْمُرُونِّي أَعْبُدُ أَيُّهَا الْجَاهِلُونَ﴾ ذَكَرُوا فِي سَبَبِ نُزُولِهَا مَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ وَغَيْرُهُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا أَنَّهُ قَالَ] : إِنَّ الْمُشْرِكِينَ بِجَهْلِهِمْ دَعَوْا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ إلى عِبَادَةِ آلِهَتِهِمْ، وَيَعْبُدُوا مَعَهُ إِلَهَهُ، فَنَزَلَتْ: ﴿قُلْ أَفَغَيْرَ اللَّهِ تَأْمُرُونِّي أَعْبُدُ أَيُّهَا الْجَاهِلُونَ وَلَقَدْ أُوحِيَ إِلَيْكَ وَإِلَى الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ لَئِنْ أَشْرَكْتَ لَيَحْبَطَنَّ عَمَلُكَ وَلَتَكُونَنَّ مِنَ الْخَاسِرِينَ﴾

وَهَذِهِ كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلَوْ أَشْرَكُوا لَحَبِطَ عَنْهُمْ مَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:٨٨] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿بَلِ اللَّهَ فَاعْبُدْ وَكُنْ مِنَ الشَّاكِرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: أَخْلِصِ الْعِبَادَةَ لِلَّهِ وَحْدَهُ، لا شريك له، أنت وَمَنْ مَعَكَ، أَنْتَ وَمَنِ اتَّبَعَكَ وَصَدَّقَكَ.

---

## 39:67 — verse 67

### Translation

The Almighty says: the polytheists did not measure Allah with His true measure, when they worshipped others alongside Him, while He is the Magnificent, than whom there is nothing more magnificent, the One capable over all things, the Possessor of all things, and all things are beneath His subjugation and His power.

Mujahid said: it was revealed concerning Quraysh. Al-Suddi said: they did not magnify Him with His true magnitude.

Muhammad ibn Ka'b said: had they measured Him with His true measure, they would not have denied Him.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas [may Allah be pleased with them both]: {And they did not measure Allah with His true measure}, they are the disbelievers who did not believe in Allah's [the Almighty's] power over them. So whoever believes that Allah is capable over all things has indeed measured Allah with His true measure, and whoever does not believe that has not measured Allah with His true measure.

Many hadiths have come related to this noble verse, and the approach in them and in similar matters is the path of the Salaf (early generations), which is to let them pass as they came, without asking "how" and without distortion.

Al-Bukhari said, regarding His saying {And they did not measure Allah with His true measure}: [chain] Abdullah ibn Mas'ud said: A rabbi from among the rabbis came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and said, "O Muhammad, we find that Allah, Mighty and Majestic, places the heavens upon a finger, the earths upon a finger, the trees upon a finger, the water and the moist earth upon a finger, and the rest of creation upon a finger, then He says: I am the King." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ laughed until his molars appeared, confirming the rabbi's statement. Then the Messenger of Allah ﷺ recited: {And they did not measure Allah with His true measure, while the earth entirely will be within His grip on the Day of Resurrection} the verse.

Al-Bukhari also related it in another place in his Sahih, as did Imam Ahmad, Muslim, al-Tirmidhi, and al-Nasa'i in the Tafsir sections of their Sunans, all of them through the hadith of Sulayman ibn Mihran al-A'mash, from Ibrahim, from Ubaydah, from [Abdullah] ibn Mas'ud, may Allah be pleased with him, with similar wording.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abdullah, may Allah be pleased with him, said: A man from the People of the Book came to the Prophet ﷺ and said, "O Abu al-Qasim, I have information reaching you that Allah [the Almighty] carries the creation upon a finger, the heavens upon a finger, the earths upon a finger, the trees upon a finger, and the moist earth upon a finger?" He said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ laughed until his molars appeared. He said: And Allah, Mighty and Majestic, revealed: {And they did not measure Allah with His true measure} to the end of the verse.

Al-Bukhari, Muslim, and al-Nasa'i related it likewise, through various chains, from al-A'mash with this content.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Ibn Abbas said: A Jew passed by the Messenger of Allah ﷺ while he was sitting, and said, "What do you say, O Abu al-Qasim, about the day when Allah will place the sky upon this," pointing with his index finger, "and the earth upon this, and the mountains upon this, and the rest of creation upon this," each time pointing with his finger. He said: So Allah, Mighty and Majestic, revealed: {And they did not measure Allah with His true measure} the verse.

Al-Tirmidhi related it likewise in the Tafsir section, from Abdullah ibn Abd al-Rahman al-Darimi, from Muhammad ibn al-Salt, from Abu Ja'far, from Abu Kudaynah Yahya ibn al-Muhallab, from Ata ibn al-Sa'ib, from Abu al-Duha Muslim ibn Subayh, with this content, and he said: hasan sahih gharib (a sound, authentic, singular report), we do not know it except through this route.

Then al-Bukhari said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, said: I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "Allah will seize the earth and fold up the heaven with His right hand, then He will say: I am the King, where are the kings of the earth?"

He related it uniquely through this route, and Muslim related it through another route.

Al-Bukhari said, in another place: [chain] Ibn Umar, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, who said: "Indeed Allah will seize the earths upon a finger on the Day of Resurrection, and the heavens will be in His right hand, then He will say: I am the King."

He related it uniquely through this route as well, and Muslim related it through another route. Imam Ahmad related it through another chain with different, more detailed and lengthier wording, saying:

[chain] Ibn Umar reported that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ recited this verse one day upon the pulpit: {And they did not measure Allah with His true measure, while the earth entirely will be within His grip on the Day of Resurrection, and the heavens will be folded in His right hand. Exalted is He and high above what they associate with Him} while the Messenger of Allah ﷺ was moving his hand like this, bringing it forward and back: "The Lord glorifies Himself: I am the Compeller, I am the Proud, I am the King, I am the Mighty, I am the Generous." Then the pulpit shook beneath the Messenger of Allah ﷺ until we said, it will surely collapse with him.

Muslim, al-Nasa'i, and Ibn Majah related it from the hadith of Abd al-Aziz ibn Abi Hazim, Muslim adding: and Ya'qub ibn Abd al-Rahman, both of them from Abu Hazim, from Ubaydullah ibn Miqsam, from Ibn Umar, with similar content.

Muslim's wording, from Ubaydullah ibn Miqsam in this hadith, is: that he looked at Abdullah ibn Umar as he narrated how the Prophet ﷺ said: Allah will take His heavens and His earths in His hand and say: I am the King, closing His fingers and opening them: I am the King, until I looked at the pulpit shaking from its lowest part, until I said, will it collapse with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ?

Al-Bazzar said: [chain] Muhammad ibn al-Munkadir said: Abdullah ibn Umar [may Allah be pleased with them both] narrated to us that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ recited this verse upon the pulpit: {And they did not measure Allah with His true measure} until he reached: {Exalted is He and high above what they associate with Him}, and the pulpit did like this, coming and going three times.

The Hafiz Imam Abu al-Qasim al-Tabarani related it from the hadith of Ubayd ibn Umayr, from Abdullah ibn Amr, and said: sahih (authentic).

Al-Tabarani said in al-Mu'jam al-Kabir: [chain] Jarir said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said to a group of his Companions: "I am about to recite to you verses from the end of Surat al-Zumar; whoever among you weeps, Paradise becomes obligatory for him." So he recited from His saying: {And they did not measure Allah with His true measure} to the end of the surah. Some of us wept, and some of us did not weep. Those who did not weep said, "O Messenger of Allah, we have striven to weep but could not." He said: "I shall recite it to you again, and whoever does not weep, let him pretend to weep." This is a hadith that is extremely gharib (singular/rare).

Even more gharib than that is what he related in al-Mu'jam al-Kabir as well: [chain] Abu Malik al-Ash'ari said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Allah the Almighty says: Three matters I have concealed from My servants; had a man seen them he would never have done evil again: had I lifted My veil so that he saw Me, so that they would become certain and know how I deal with My creation when I come to them, and I seize the heavens with My hand, then I seize the earth and the earths, then I say: I am the King, who has dominion besides Me? Then I show them Paradise and what I have prepared for them therein of every good thing, so that they become certain of it. And I show them the Fire and what I have prepared for them therein of every evil thing, so that they become certain of it. But I have deliberately concealed that from them, so that I may know how they act, though I have made it clear to them."

This is a chain that is close in reliability, and it is a version through which many hadiths are related. And Allah knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: وَمَا قَدَّرَ الْمُشْرِكُونَ اللَّهَ حَقَّ قَدْرِهِ، حِينَ عَبَدُوا مَعَهُ غَيْرَهُ، وَهُوَ الْعَظِيمُ الَّذِي لَا أَعْظَمَ مِنْهُ، الْقَادِرُ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ، الْمَالِكُ لِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ، وَكُلُّ شَيْءٍ تَحْتَ قَهْرِهِ وَقُدْرَتِهِ.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: نَزَلَتْ فِي قُرَيْشٍ. وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: مَا عَظَّمُوهُ حَقَّ عَظَمَتِهِ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ: لَوْ قَدَّرُوهُ حَقَّ قَدْرِهِ مَا كَذَّبُوهُ.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا] : ﴿وَمَا قَدَرُوا اللَّهَ حَقَّ قَدْرِهِ﴾ هُمُ الْكُفَّارُ الَّذِينَ لَمْ يُؤْمِنُوا بِقُدْرَةِ اللَّهِ [تَعَالَى] عَلَيْهِمْ، فَمَنْ آمَنَ أن الله على كل شي قَدِيرٌ، فَقَدْ قَدَرَ اللَّهُ حَقَّ قَدْرِهِ، وَمَنْ لَمْ يُؤْمِنْ بِذَلِكَ فَلَمْ يُقَدِّرِ اللَّهَ حَقَّ قَدْرِهِ.

وَقَدْ وَرَدَتْ أَحَادِيثُ كَثِيرَةٌ مُتَعَلِّقَةٌ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ، وَالطَّرِيقُ فِيهَا وَفِي أَمْثَالِهَا مَذْهَبُ السَّلَفِ، وَهُوَ إِمْرَارُهَا كَمَا جَاءَتْ مِنْ غَيْرِ تَكْيِيفٍ وَلَا تَحْرِيفٍ.

قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا قَدَرُوا اللَّهَ حَقَّ قَدْرِهِ﴾ حَدَّثَنَا آدَمُ، حَدَّثَنَا شَيْبَانُ، عَنْ مَنْصُورٍ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَنْ عُبَيْدَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ قَالَ: جَاءَ حَبْرٌ مِنَ الْأَحْبَارِ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقَالَ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ: إِنَّا نجد أن الله عز وجل يجعل السموات عَلَى إِصْبَعٍ، وَالْأَرْضِينَ عَلَى إِصْبَعٍ، وَالشَّجَرَ عَلَى إِصْبَعٍ، وَالْمَاءَ وَالثَّرَى عَلَى إِصْبَعٍ، وَسَائِرَ الْخَلَائِقِ عَلَى إِصْبَعٍ. فَيَقُولُ: أَنَا الْمَلِكُ. فَضَحِكَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ حَتَّى بَدَتْ نَوَاجِذُهُ، تَصْدِيقًا لِقَوْلِ الْحَبْرِ، ثُمَّ قَرَأَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: ﴿وَمَا قَدَرُوا اللَّهَ حَقَّ قَدْرِهِ وَالأرْضُ جَمِيعًا قَبْضَتُهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ﴾ الْآيَةَ .

وَ [قَدْ] رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ أَيْضًا فِي غَيْرِ هَذَا الْمَوْضِعِ مِنْ صَحِيحِهِ، وَالْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، وَمُسْلِمٌ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ وَالنَّسَائِيُّ فِي التَّفْسِيرِ مِنْ سَنَنَيْهِمَا، كُلُّهُمْ مِنْ حَدِيثِ سُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ مِهْرَانَ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ عَنْ عُبَيْدَةَ، عَنْ [عَبْدِ اللَّهِ] ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، بِنَحْوِهِ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا الأعمش، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ عَنْ عَلْقَمَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: جَاءَ رَجُلٌ إِلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ مَنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ، فَقَالَ: يَا أَبَا الْقَاسِمِ، أُبَلِّغَكَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ [تَعَالَى] يَحْمِلُ الْخَلَائِقَ عَلَى إِصْبَعٍ، والسموات عَلَى إِصْبَعٍ، وَالْأَرْضِينَ عَلَى إِصْبَعٍ، وَالشَّجَرَ عَلَى إِصْبَعٍ، وَالثَّرَى عَلَى إِصْبَعٍ؟ قَالَ: فَضَحِكَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ حَتَّى بَدَتْ نَوَاجِذُهُ. قَالَ: وَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿وَمَا قَدَرُوا اللَّهَ حَقَّ قَدْرِهِ﴾ إِلَى آخِرِ الْآيَةِ.

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ، وَمُسْلِمٌ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ -مِنْ طُرُقٍ-عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ بِهِ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا حُسَيْنُ بْنُ حَسَنٍ الْأَشْقَرُ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو كُدَيْنَةَ، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ عَنْ أَبِي الضُّحَى، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: مَرَّ يَهُودِيٌّ بِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَهُوَ جَالِسٌ فَقَالَ: كَيْفَ تَقُولُ يَا أَبَا الْقَاسِمِ: يَوْمَ يَجْعَلُ اللَّهُ السَّمَاءَ عَلَى ذِهْ -وَأَشَارَ بِالسَّبَّابَةِ-وَالْأَرْضَ عَلَى ذِهْ، وَالْجِبَالَ عَلَى ذِهِ وَسَائِرَ الْخَلْقِ عَلَى ذِهْ -كُلُّ ذَلِكَ يُشِيرُ بِإِصْبُعِهِ -قَالَ: فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿وَمَا قَدَرُوا اللَّهَ حَقَّ قَدْرِهِ﴾ الْآيَةَ.

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ فِي التَّفْسِيرِ عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ الدَّارِمِيِّ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ الصَّلْت، عَنْ أَبِي جَعْفَرٍ، عَنْ أَبِي كُدَيْنَةَ يَحْيَى بْنُ الْمُهَلَّبِ، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ السَّائِبِ، عَنْ أَبِي الضُّحَى مُسْلِمُ بْنُ صُبَيْحٍ، بِهِ ، وَقَالَ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ غَرِيبٌ، لَا نَعْرِفُهُ إِلَّا مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ عُفَيْرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا اللَّيْثُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ خَالِدِ بْنِ مُسَافِرٍ، عَنِ ابْنُ شِهَابٍ، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ: أَنَّ أَبَا هُرَيْرَةَ ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: يَقْبِضُ اللَّهُ الْأَرْضَ، وَيَطْوِي السَّمَاءَ بِيَمِينِهِ، ثُمَّ يَقُولُ: أَنَا الْمَلِكُ، أَيْنَ مُلُوكُ الْأَرْضِ".

تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ ، وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ .

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ -فِي مَوْضِعٍ آخَرَ-: حَدَّثَنَا مُقَدَّم بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَمِّي الْقَاسِمُ بْنُ يَحْيَى، عَنْ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ، عَنْ نَافِعٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَقْبِضُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ الْأَرْضِينَ على إصبع، وتكون السموات بِيَمِينِهِ، ثُمَّ يَقُولُ: أَنَا الْمَلِكُ".

تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ أَيْضًا مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ ، وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ . وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ مِنْ طَرِيقٍ أُخْرَى بِلَفْظٍ آخَرَ أَبْسَطَ مِنْ هَذَا السِّيَاقِ وَأَطْوَلَ، فَقَالَ:

حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، أَخْبَرَنَا إِسْحَاقُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنْ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مِقْسَمٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَرَأَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ ذَاتَ يَوْمٍ عَلَى الْمِنْبَرِ: ﴿وَمَا قَدَرُوا اللَّهَ حَقَّ قَدْرِهِ وَالأرْضُ جَمِيعًا قَبْضَتُهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَالسَّموَاتُ مَطْوِيَّاتٌ بِيَمِينِهِ سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى عَمَّا يُشْرِكُونَ﴾ وَرَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ هَكَذَا بِيَدِهِ، يُحَرِّكُهَا يُقْبِلُ بِهَا وَيُدْبِرُ: "يُمَجِّدُ الرَّبُّ نفسه: أنا الجبار، أنا المتكبر، أنا الْمَلِكُ، أَنَا الْعَزِيزُ، أَنَا الْكَرِيمُ". فَرَجَفَ بِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ الْمِنْبَرُ حَتَّى قُلْنَا: لَيَخِرَّن بِهِ.

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ بْنِ أَبِي حَازِمٍ -زَادَ مُسْلِمٌ: وَيَعْقُوبُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، كِلَاهُمَا عَنْ أَبِي حَازِمٍ، عَنْ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مِقْسَمٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ، بِهِ، نَحْوَهُ .

وَلَفْظُ مُسْلِمٍ -عَنْ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مِقْسَمٍ فِي هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ-: أَنَّهُ نَظَرَ إِلَى عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ كَيْفَ يَحْكِي النَّبِيُّ ﷺ، قَالَ: يَأْخُذُ اللَّهُ سمواته وَأَرْضِيهِ بِيَدِهِ وَيَقُولُ: أَنَا الْمَلِكُ، وَيَقْبِضُ أَصَابِعَهُ وَيَبْسُطُهَا: أَنَا الْمَلِكُ، حَتَّى نَظَرْتُ إِلَى الْمِنْبَرِ يَتَحَرَّكُ مِنْ أَسْفَلِ شَيْءٍ مِنْهُ، حَتَّى إِنِّي لَأَقُولَ: أَسَاقِطٌ هُوَ بِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ؟.

وَقَالَ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ سَيْفٍ ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَلِيٍّ الْحَنَفِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبَّادٌ المنْقرَي، حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْمُنْكَدِرِ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا] ، أن رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم قَرَأَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ عَلَى الْمِنْبَرِ: ﴿وَمَا قَدَرُوا اللَّهَ حَقَّ قَدْرِهِ﴾ حَتَّى بَلَغَ: ﴿سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى عَمَّا يُشْرِكُونَ﴾ ، فَقَالَ الْمِنْبَرُ هَكَذَا، فَجَاءَ وَذَهَبَ ثَلَاثَ مَرَّاتٍ .

وَرَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عُبَيْدِ بْنِ عُمَيْرٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، وَقَالَ: صَحِيحٌ .

وَقَالَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ فِي الْمُعْجَمِ الْكَبِيرِ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ مُعَاوِيَةَ العُتْبي، حَدَّثَنَا حَيَّانُ بْنُ نَافِعِ بْنِ صَخْرِ بْنِ جُوَيْرِيَّةَ، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ سَالِمٍ الْقَدَّاحُ، عَنْ مَعْمَرِ بْنِ الْحَسَنِ، عَنْ بَكْرِ بْنِ خُنَيْس، عَنْ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ بْنِ عُمَيْرٍ، عَنْ جَرِيرٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم لِنَفِرٍ مِنْ أَصْحَابِهِ: "إِنِّي قَارِئٌ عَلَيْكُمْ آيَاتٍ مِنْ آخِرِ سُورَةِ الزُّمَرِ، فَمَنْ بَكَى مِنْكُمْ وَجَبَتْ لَهُ الْجَنَّةُ"؟ فَقَرَأَهَا مِنْ عِنْدِ قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَا قَدَرُوا اللَّهَ حَقَّ قَدْرِهِ﴾ ، إِلَى آخِرِ السُّورَةِ، فَمِنَّا مَنْ بَكَى، وَمِنَّا مَنْ لَمْ يَبْكِ، فَقَالَ الَّذِينَ لَمْ يَبْكُوا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ لَقَدْ جَهِدْنَا أَنْ نَبْكِيَ فَلَمْ نَبْكِ؟ فَقَالَ: "إِنِّي سَأَقْرَؤُهَا عَلَيْكُمْ فَمَنْ لَمْ يَبْكِ فَلْيَتَبَاكَ". هَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ جِدًّا .

وَأَغْرَبُ مِنْهُ مَا رَوَاهُ فِي الْمُعْجَمِ الْكَبِيرِ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا هَاشِمُ بْنُ مُرْثَد ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ عَيَّاشٍ، حَدَّثَنِي أَبِي، حَدَّثَنِي ضَمْضَمُ بْنُ زُرْعَةَ، عَنْ شُرَيْحِ بْنِ عُبَيْدٍ، عَنْ أبي مالك الْأَشْعَرِيِّ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يَقُولُ: ثَلَاثُ خِلَالٍ غَيَّبتُهُنَّ عَنْ عِبَادِي، لَوْ رَآهُنَّ رَجُلٌ مَا عَمِلَ سُوءًا أَبَدًا: لَوْ كَشَفْتُ غِطَائِي فرآني حتى نستيقن وَيَعْلَمَ كَيْفَ أَفْعَلُ بِخَلْقِي إِذَا أَتَيْتُهُمْ، وَقَبَضْتُ السموات بِيَدِي، ثُمَّ قَبَضْتُ الْأَرْضَ وَالْأَرْضِينَ، ثُمَّ قُلْتُ: أَنَا الْمَلِكُ، مَنْ ذَا الَّذِي لَهُ الْمُلْكُ دُونِي؟ ثُمَّ أَرَيْتُهُمُ الْجَنَّةَ وَمَا أَعْدَدْتُ لَهُمْ فِيهَا مِنْ كُلِّ خَيْرٍ، فَيَسْتَيْقِنُوهَا. وَأُرِيهِمُ النَّارَ وَمَا أَعْدَدْتُ لَهُمْ فِيهَا مِنْ كُلِّ شَرٍّ فَيَسْتَيْقِنُوهَا، وَلَكِنْ عَمْدًا غَيَّبْتُ ذَلِكَ عَنْهُمْ لِأَعْلَمَ كَيْفَ يَعْمَلُونَ، وَقَدْ بَيَّنْتُهُ لَهُمْ" .

وَهَذَا إِسْنَادٌ مُتَقَارِبٌ، وَهِيَ نُسْخَةٌ تُرْوَى بِهَا أَحَادِيثُ جَمَّةٌ، والله أعلم.

---

## 39:68-70 — verses 68-70 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing about the terror of the Day of Resurrection and the mighty signs and terrifying convulsions that will occur on it. His saying: {And the Trumpet will be blown, and whoever is in the heavens and whoever is on the earth will fall dead, except whom Allah wills}. This blowing is the second blowing, the blowing of stunning (al-sa'q), and it is the one by which the living among the inhabitants of the heavens and the earth die, except whom Allah wills, as is explicitly stated and explained in the well-known hadith of the Trumpet. Then He seizes the souls of those who remain, until the last one to die is the Angel of Death, and the Ever-Living, the Self-Subsisting (al-Hayy al-Qayyum), who existed first and who remains last, remains alone in everlasting continuance and permanence. And He says: {To whom belongs the dominion this Day?} [Ghafir: 16], three times. Then He answers Himself, saying: {To Allah, the One, the Subduer}, that is, the One who is one and who has subdued everything and decreed annihilation upon everything. Then He gives life first to Israfil, and commands him to blow into the Trumpet again, which is the third blowing, the blowing of resurrection. The Almighty said: {Then it will be blown again, and behold, they will be standing, looking on}, meaning alive after having been bones and scattered remains, they become alive, looking upon the terrors of the Day of Resurrection, as the Almighty said: {Then it will be but one blast, and behold, they will be on the surface of the earth} [al-Nazi'at: 13-14], and the Almighty said: {The Day He will call you and you will respond with His praise, and you will think that you had remained but a little} [al-Isra: 52], and the Almighty said: {And among His signs is that the heaven and earth stand by His command. Then when He calls you with a single call from the earth, behold, you will come forth} [al-Rum: 25].

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Ya'qub ibn Asim ibn Urwah ibn Mas'ud said: I heard a man say to Abdullah ibn Amr: "You say that the Hour will occur at such and such a time?" He said: "I had resolved not to tell you anything. I only said: You will soon see, after a little while, a mighty matter." Then Abdullah ibn Amr said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The Dajjal will emerge among my nation, and he will remain among them forty, I do not know whether forty days, forty years, forty months, or forty nights, then Allah will send Isa the son of Maryam (peace be upon him), as if he were Urwah ibn Mas'ud al-Thaqafi, and he will appear and Allah will destroy him. Then the people will remain after him for seven years, with no enmity between any two of them. Then Allah will send a cold wind from the direction of Syria, and no one will remain who has even the weight of a mote of faith in his heart except that it will take him, even if one of them were in the depths of a mountain, it would reach him." He said: I heard this from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ: "And the worst of people will remain, as light as birds and with the intelligence of beasts, recognizing no good and disapproving of no evil." He said: "Then Satan will appear to them in a form and say: 'Will you not respond?' And he will command them to worship idols, and they will worship them, and during that time their provision will be abundant and their life good. Then the Trumpet will be blown, and no one will hear it except that he will incline his ear toward it, and the first to hear it will be a man plastering his water trough, and he will be struck down (yus'aq), and then no one will remain except that he is struck down. Then Allah will send, or Allah will send down, rain like dew, or like shade, Nu'man was uncertain, and from it the bodies of people will sprout. Then it will be blown a second time, and behold, they will be standing, looking on. Then it will be said: 'O people, come to your Lord': {Stop them, for they are to be questioned} [al-Saffat: 24]." He said: "Then it will be said: 'Bring forth the contingent of the Fire.'" He said: "It will be asked: 'How many?' And it will be said: 'From every thousand, nine hundred and ninety-nine.' On that day children will be raised up gray-haired, and on that day the Shin will be uncovered."

Muslim alone narrated this in his Sahih.

Al-Bukhari said: [chain] al-A'mash said: I heard Abu Salih say: I heard Abu Hurayrah [may Allah be pleased with him] from the Prophet ﷺ say: "Between the two blowings will be forty." They said: "O Abu Hurayrah, forty days?" He said: "I refuse to say." They said: "Forty years?" He said: "I refuse." They said: "Forty months?" He said: "I refuse. And everything of the human being will decay except the coccyx (ajb al-dhanab, the tailbone), from which creation will be reassembled."

Abu Ya'la said: [chain] Isma'il ibn Ayyash, from Umar ibn Muhammad, from Zayd ibn Aslam, from his father, from Abu Hurayrah [may Allah be pleased with him], from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "I asked Gabriel (peace be upon him) about this verse: {And the Trumpet will be blown, and whoever is in the heavens and whoever is on the earth will fall dead, except whom Allah wills}, who are those whom Allah did not will to strike down? He said: 'They are the martyrs, girded with their swords around His Throne. The angels of the Day of Resurrection will meet them and bring them to the place of gathering upon mounts of ruby whose markings are softer than silk, whose stride spans as far as the eye of a man can see. They will travel through Paradise, saying during the length of their excursion: Let us go to our Lord, Mighty and Majestic, that we may see how He judges between His creation. My God will smile upon them, and if He smiles upon a servant in any station, no reckoning will be held against him.'"

All of its narrators are trustworthy except the shaykh of Isma'il ibn Ayyash, who is unknown. And Allah knows best.

His saying: {And the earth will shine with the light of its Lord}, meaning it will be illuminated on the Day of Resurrection when the Truth, Blessed and Exalted, manifests Himself to creation for the passing of judgment. {And the Record will be placed}: Qatadah said, the record of deeds. {And the prophets will be brought}: Ibn Abbas said, they will bear witness against the nations that they conveyed to them the messages of Allah. {And the witnesses}: meaning the witnesses among the angels who record the deeds of the servants, of good and evil. {And it will be judged between them in truth}, meaning with justice, {and they will not be wronged}. Allah [the Almighty] said: {And We place the scales of justice for the Day of Resurrection, so no soul will be wronged at all. Even if it be the weight of a mustard seed, We will bring it forth, and sufficient are We as reckoners} [al-Anbiya: 47], and Allah [the Almighty] said: {And if there is a good deed, He will multiply it and give from Himself a great reward} [al-Nisa: 40]. And it is for this reason He said: {And every soul will be paid in full for what it did}, meaning of good or evil, {and He is most knowing of what they do}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ هَوْلِ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ، وَمَا يَكُونُ فِيهِ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ الْعَظِيمَةِ وَالزَّلَازِلِ الْهَائِلَةِ، فَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَنُفِخَ فِي الصُّورِ فَصَعِقَ مَنْ فِي السَّمَوَاتِ وَمَنْ فِي الأرْضِ إِلا مَنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ﴾ ، هَذِهِ النَّفْخَةُ هِيَ الثَّانِيَةُ، وَهِيَ نَفْخَةُ الصَّعْقِ، وَهِيَ الَّتِي يموت بها الأحياء من أهل السموات وَالْأَرْضِ، إِلَّا مَنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ كَمَا هُوَ مُصَرَّحٌ بِهِ مُفَسَّرًا فِي حَدِيثِ الصُّورِ الْمَشْهُورِ. ثُمَّ يَقْبِضُ أَرْوَاحَ الْبَاقِينَ حَتَّى يَكُونَ آخِرُ مَنْ يَمُوتُ مَلَكَ الْمَوْتِ، وَيَنْفَرِدُ الْحَيُّ الْقَيُّومُ الَّذِي كَانَ أَوَّلًا وَهُوَ الْبَاقِي آخِرًا بِالدَّيْمُومَةِ وَالْبَقَاءِ، وَيَقُولُ: ﴿لِمَنِ الْمُلْكُ الْيَوْمَ﴾ [غَافِرٍ:١٦] ثَلَاثَ مَرَّاتٍ. ثُمَّ يُجِيبُ نَفْسَهُ بِنَفْسِهِ فَيَقُولُ: ﴿لِلَّهِ الْوَاحِدِ الْقَهَّارِ﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِي هُوَ وَاحِدٌ وَقَدْ قَهَرَ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ، وَحَكَمَ بِالْفَنَاءِ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ. ثُمَّ يُحْيِي أَوَّلَ مَنْ يُحْيِي إِسْرَافِيلَ، وَيَأْمُرُهُ أَنْ يُنْفَخَ فِي الصُّورِ أُخْرَى، وَهِيَ النَّفْخَةُ الثَّالِثَةُ نَفْخَةُ الْبَعْثِ، قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿ثُمَّ نُفِخَ فِيهِ أُخْرَى فَإِذَا هُمْ قِيَامٌ يَنْظُرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: أَحْيَاءٌ بَعْدَ مَا كَانُوا عِظَامًا وَرُفَاتًا، صَارُوا أَحْيَاءً يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَى أَهْوَالِ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَإِنَّمَا هِيَ زَجْرَةٌ وَاحِدَةٌ فَإِذَا هُمْ بِالسَّاهِرَةِ﴾ [النَّازِعَاتِ:١٤، ١٣] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ يَدْعُوكُمْ فَتَسْتَجِيبُونَ بِحَمْدِهِ وَتَظُنُّونَ إِنْ لَبِثْتُمْ إِلا قَلِيلا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ:٥٢] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمِنْ آيَاتِهِ أَنْ تَقُومَ السَّمَاءُ وَالأرْضُ بِأَمْرِهِ ثُمَّ إِذَا دَعَاكُمْ دَعْوَةً مِنَ الأرْضِ إِذَا أَنْتُمْ تَخْرُجُونَ﴾ [الرُّومِ:٢٥] .

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنِ النُّعْمَانِ بْنِ سَالِمٍ قَالَ: سمعت يَعْقُوبَ بْنَ عَاصِمِ بْنِ عُرْوَةَ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ رَجُلًا قَالَ لِعَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو : إِنَّكَ تَقُولُ: السَّاعَةُ تَقُومُ إِلَى كَذَا وَكَذَا؟ قَالَ: لَقَدْ هَمَمْتُ أَلَّا أُحَدِّثَكُمْ شَيْئًا، إِنَّمَا قُلْتُ: سَتَرَوْنَ بَعْدَ قَلِيلٍ أَمْرًا عَظِيمًا. ثُمَّ قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عَمْرٍو: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يَخْرُجُ الدَّجَّالُ فِي أُمَّتِي، فَيَمْكُثُ فِيهِمْ أَرْبَعِينَ-لَا أَدْرِي أَرْبَعِينَ يَوْمًا أَوْ أَرْبَعِينَ عَامًا أَوْ أَرْبَعِينَ شَهْرًا أَوْ أَرْبَعِينَ لَيْلَةً -فَيَبْعَثُ اللَّهُ عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ ، كَأَنَّهُ عُرْوَةُ بْنُ مَسْعُودٍ الثَّقَفِيُّ، فَيَظْهَرُ فَيُهْلِكُهُ اللَّهُ . ثُمَّ يَلْبَثُ النَّاسُ بَعْدَهُ سِنِينَ سَبْعًا لَيْسَ بَيْنَ اثْنَيْنِ عَدَاوَةٌ، ثُمَّ يُرْسِلُ اللَّهُ رِيحًا بَارِدَةً مِنْ قِبَلِ الشَّامِ، فَلَا يَبْقَى أَحَدٌ فِي قَلْبِهِ مِثْقَالُ ذَرَّةٍ مِنْ إِيمَانٍ إِلَّا قَبَضَتْهُ، حَتَّى لَوْ أَنَّ أَحَدَهُمْ كَانَ فِي كَبِدِ جَبَلٍ لَدَخَلَتْ عَلَيْهِ". قَالَ: سَمِعْتُهَا مِنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "وَيَبْقَى شِرَارُ النَّاسِ فِي خِفَّةِ الطَّيْرِ، وَأَحْلَامِ السِّبَاعِ، لَا يَعْرِفُونَ مَعْرُوفًا، وَلَا يُنْكِرُونَ مُنْكَرًا". قَالَ: "فَيَتَمَثَّلُ لَهُمُ الشَّيْطَانُ فَيَقُولُ: أَلَا تَسْتَجِيبُونَ؟ فَيَأْمُرُهُمْ بِالْأَوْثَانِ فَيَعْبُدُونَهَا، وَهُمْ فِي ذَلِكَ دَارَّةٌ أَرْزَاقُهُمْ، حَسَنٌ عَيْشُهُمْ. ثُمَّ يُنْفَخُ فِي الصُّورِ فَلَا يَسْمَعُهُ أَحَدٌ إِلَّا أَصْغَى لَهُ، وَأَوَّلُ مَنْ يَسْمَعُهُ رَجُلٌ يَلُوطُ حَوْضَهُ، فَيُصْعَقُ، ثُمَّ لَا يَبْقَى أَحَدٌ إِلَّا صُعِقَ. ثُمَّ يُرْسِلُ اللَّهُ -أَوْ: يُنْزِلُ اللَّهُ مَطَرًا كَأَنَّهُ الطَّلُّ-أَوِ الظِّلُّ شَكَّ نُعْمَانُ -فَتَنْبُتُ مِنْهُ أَجْسَادُ النَّاسِ. ثُمَّ يُنْفَخُ فِيهِ أُخْرَى فَإِذَا هُمْ قِيَامٌ يَنْظُرُونَ، ثُمَّ يُقَالُ: يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ، هَلُمُّوا إِلَى رَبِّكُمْ: ﴿وَقِفُوهُمْ إِنَّهُمْ مَسْئُولُونَ﴾ [الصَّافَّاتِ:٢٤] ، قَالَ: "ثُمَّ يُقَالُ: أَخْرِجُوا بَعْثَ النَّارِ". قَالَ: "فَيُقَالُ: كَمْ؟ فَيُقَالُ: مِنْ كُلِّ أَلْفٍ تِسْعَمِائَةٍ وَتِسْعَةً وَتِسْعِينَ فَيَوْمَئِذٍ تُبْعَثُ الْوِلْدَانُ شِيبًا، وَيَوْمَئِذٍ يُكْشَفُ عَنْ سَاقٍ".

انْفَرَدَ بِإِخْرَاجِهِ مُسْلِمٌ فِي صَحِيحِهِ .

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا عُمَرُ بْنُ حَفْصِ بْنِ غِيَاثٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ أَبَا صَالِحٍ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ أَبَا هُرَيْرَةَ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "بَيْنَ النَّفْخَتَيْنِ أَرْبَعُونَ" . قَالُوا: يَا أَبَا هُرَيْرَةَ، أَرْبَعُونَ يَوْمًا؟ قَالَ: أَبَيْتُ، قَالُوا: أَرْبَعُونَ سَنَةً؟ قَالَ: أبي، قَالُوا: أَرْبَعُونَ شَهْرًا؟ قَالَ: أَبَيْتُ، وَيَبْلَى كُلُّ شَيْءٍ مِنَ الْإِنْسَانِ إِلَّا عَجْبُ ذَنَبِهِ فِيهِ يُرَكَّبُ الْخَلْقُ .

وَقَالَ أَبُو يَعْلَى: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ مَعِينٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْيَمَانِ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ عَيَّاشٍ، عَنْ عُمَرَ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "سَأَلْتُ جِبْرِيلَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، عَنْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿وَنُفِخَ فِي الصُّورِ فَصَعِقَ مَنْ فِي السَّمَوَاتِ وَمَنْ فِي الأرْضِ إِلا مَنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ﴾ مَنِ الَّذِينَ لَمْ يَشَأِ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَصْعَقَهُمْ؟ قَالَ: هُمُ الشُّهَدَاءُ، مُقَلِّدُونَ أَسْيَافَهُمْ حَوْلَ عَرْشِهِ، تَتَلَقَّاهُمْ مَلَائِكَةُ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ إِلَى الْمَحْشَرِ بِنَجَائِبَ مِنْ يَاقُوتٍ نِمَارُهَا أَلْيَنُ مِنَ الْحَرِيرِ، مَدُّ خُطَاهَا مَدُّ أَبْصَارِ الرِّجَالِ، يَسِيرُونَ فِي الْجَنَّةِ يَقُولُونَ عِنْدَ طُولِ النُّزْهَةِ: انْطَلَقُوا بِنَا إِلَى رَبِّنَا، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، لِنَنْظُرَ كَيْفَ يَقْضِي بَيْنَ خَلْقِهِ، يَضْحَكُ إِلَيْهِمْ إِلَهِي، وَإِذَا ضَحِكَ إِلَى عَبْدٍ فِي مَوْطِنٍ فلا حساب عليه".

رِجَالُهُ كُلُّهُمْ ثِقَاتٌ إِلَّا شَيْخَ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ عَيَّاشٍ، فَإِنَّهُ غَيْرُ مَعْرُوفٍ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَأَشْرَقَتِ الأرْضُ بِنُورِ رَبِّهَا﴾ أَيْ: أَضَاءَتْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ إِذَا تَجَلَّى الْحَقُّ، تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى، لِلْخَلَائِقِ لِفَصْلِ الْقَضَاءِ، ﴿وَوُضِعَ الْكِتَابُ﴾ قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: كِتَابُ الْأَعْمَالِ، ﴿وَجِيءَ بِالنَّبِيِّينَ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: يَشْهَدُونَ عَلَى الْأُمَمِ بِأَنَّهُمْ بَلَّغُوهُمْ رِسَالَاتِ اللَّهِ إِلَيْهِمْ، ﴿وَالشُّهَدَاءِ﴾ أَيِ: الشُّهَدَاءِ مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ الْحَفَظَةِ عَلَى أَعْمَالِ الْعِبَادِ مِنْ خَيْرٍ وَشَرٍّ، ﴿وَقُضِيَ بَيْنَهُمْ بِالْحَقِّ﴾ أَيْ: بِالْعَدْلِ ﴿وَهُمْ لَا يُظْلَمُونَ﴾ قَالَ اللَّهُ [تَعَالَى] : ﴿وَنَضَعُ الْمَوَازِينَ الْقِسْطَ لِيَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ فَلا تُظْلَمُ نَفْسٌ شَيْئًا وَإِنْ كَانَ مِثْقَالَ حَبَّةٍ مِنْ خَرْدَلٍ أَتَيْنَا بِهَا وَكَفَى بِنَا حَاسِبِينَ﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ:٤٧] ، وَقَالَ [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِنْ تَكُ حَسَنَةً يُضَاعِفْهَا وَيُؤْتِ مِنْ لَدُنْهُ أَجْرًا عَظِيمًا﴾ [النِّسَاءِ:٤٠] ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَوُفِّيَتْ كُلُّ نَفْسٍ مَا عَمِلَتْ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ خَيْرٍ أَوْ شَرٍّ ﴿وَهُوَ أَعْلَمُ بِمَا يَفْعَلُونَ﴾

---

## 39:71-72 — verses 71-72 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs of the state of the wretched disbelievers, how they will be driven to the Fire. They will be driven with a violent driving, with rebuke, threat, and warning, as the Almighty said: {The Day they are driven to the Fire of Hell with a violent driving} [al-Tur: 13], meaning they will be pushed into it forcefully. This while they are thirsty and parched, as He said in another verse: {The Day We gather the God-fearing to the Most Merciful as a delegation, and drive the criminals to Hell as a thirsty herd} [Maryam: 85-86]. And they are in that state deaf, dumb, and blind, some of them walking upon their faces: {And We will gather them on the Day of Resurrection upon their faces, blind, dumb, and deaf. Their abode is Hell; every time it subsides We increase them in blazing fire} [al-Isra: 97].

His saying: {Until, when they reach it, its gates will be opened} means, as soon as they arrive at it, its gates are opened for them swiftly, so that their punishment may be hastened upon them. Then its keepers among the zabaniyah (the guardian angels of Hell), who are harsh in temperament and severe in strength, will say to them, by way of rebuke, reproach, and castigation: {Did there not come to you messengers from among yourselves}, meaning, of your own kind, with whom you were able to converse and from whom you could take instruction, {reciting to you the verses of your Lord}, meaning, establishing against you the proofs and evidences of the truth of what they called you to, {and warning you of the meeting of this Day of yours}, meaning, cautioning you against the evil of this Day? The disbelievers will say to them: {Yes indeed}, meaning, they did come to us and warn us, and they established against us the proofs and evidences, {but the word of punishment was justly decreed upon the disbelievers},

meaning, but we denied them and opposed them, because of the wretchedness that had already been decreed for us, which we deserved, since we turned away from truth to falsehood. As the Almighty said, reporting of them in another verse: {Every time a group is thrown into it, its keepers ask them, "Did there not come to you a warner?" They say, "Yes indeed, a warner did come to us, but we denied him and said, 'God has not sent down anything; you are only in great error.'" And they will say, "If only we had listened or reasoned, we would not have been among the companions of the Blazing Fire"} [al-Mulk: 8-10], meaning, they will turn upon themselves with blame and regret, {and so they will confess their sin, so away with the companions of the Blazing Fire} [al-Mulk: 11], meaning, distance and loss be upon them.

His saying here: {It will be said, "Enter the gates of Hell, abiding therein eternally"} means, everyone who sees them and knows their state bears witness against them that they deserve the punishment. For this reason, this statement is not attributed to a specified speaker, but rather left unspecified, to indicate that all existence bears witness against them that they deserve what they are in, by virtue of what the All-Knowing, All-Just has judged concerning them. Therefore the Exalted and Mighty said: {It will be said, "Enter the gates of Hell, abiding therein eternally"}, meaning, remaining in it forever, with no exit for you from it and no departure for you from it. {How evil is the abode of the arrogant}, meaning, how evil is the final destination and how evil is the resting place for you, on account of your arrogance in the worldly life and your refusal to follow the truth. It is that very arrogance which brought you to the state you are now in. How evil is the condition, and how evil is the final end.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ حَالِ الْأَشْقِيَاءِ الْكُفَّارِ كَيْفَ يُسَاقُونَ إِلَى النَّارِ؟ وَإِنَّمَا يُسَاقُونَ سَوْقًا عَنِيفًا بِزَجْرٍ وَتَهْدِيدٍ وَوَعِيدٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ يُدَعُّونَ إِلَى نَارِ جَهَنَّمَ دَعًّا﴾ [الطُّورِ:١٣] أَيْ: يُدْفَعُونَ إِلَيْهَا دَفْعًا. هَذَا وَهُمْ عِطَاشٌ ظِمَاءٌ، كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿يَوْمَ نَحْشُرُ الْمُتَّقِينَ إِلَى الرَّحْمَنِ وَفْدًا وَنَسُوقُ الْمُجْرِمِينَ إِلَى جَهَنَّمَ وِرْدًا﴾ [مَرْيَمَ:٨٦، ٨٥] . وَهُمْ فِي تِلْكَ الْحَالِ صُمُّ وَبُكْمٌ وَعُمْيٌ، مِنْهُمْ مَنْ يَمْشِي عَلَى وَجْهِهِ، ﴿وَنَحْشُرُهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ عَلَى وُجُوهِهِمْ عُمْيًا وَبُكْمًا وَصُمًّا مَأْوَاهُمْ جَهَنَّمُ كُلَّمَا خَبَتْ زِدْنَاهُمْ سَعِيرًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ:٩٧] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا جَاءُوهَا فُتِحَتْ أَبْوَابُهَا﴾ أَيْ: بِمُجَرَّدِ وُصُولِهِمْ إِلَيْهَا فُتِحَتْ لَهُمْ أَبْوَابُهَا سَرِيعًا، لِتُعَجِّلَ لَهُمُ الْعُقُوبَةَ، ثُمَّ يَقُولُ لَهُمْ خَزَنَتُهَا مِنَ الزَّبَانِيَةِ -الَّذِينَ هُمْ غِلَاظُ الْأَخْلَاقِ، شِدَادُ الْقُوَى عَلَى وَجْهِ التَّقْرِيعِ وَالتَّوْبِيخِ وَالتَّنْكِيلِ-: ﴿أَلَمْ يَأْتِكُمْ رُسُلٌ مِنْكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ جِنْسِكُمْ تَتَمَكَّنُونَ مِنْ مُخَاطَبَتِهِمْ وَالْأَخْذِ عَنْهُمْ، ﴿يَتْلُونَ عَلَيْكُمْ آيَاتِ رَبِّكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: يُقِيمُونَ عَلَيْكُمُ الْحُجَجَ وَالْبَرَاهِينَ عَلَى صِحَّةٍ مَا دَعَوْكُمْ إِلَيْهِ، ﴿وَيُنْذِرُونَكُمْ لِقَاءَ يَوْمِكُمْ هَذَا﴾ أَيْ: وَيُحَذِّرُونَكُمْ مِنْ شَرِّ هَذَا الْيَوْمِ؟ فَيَقُولُ الْكُفَّارُ لَهُمْ: ﴿بَلَى﴾ أَيْ: قَدْ جَاءُونَا وَأَنْذَرُونَا، وَأَقَامُوا عَلَيْنَا الْحُجَجَ وَالْبَرَاهِينَ، ﴿وَلَكِنْ حَقَّتْ كَلِمَةُ الْعَذَابِ عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ﴾

أَيْ: وَلَكِنْ كَذَّبْنَاهُمْ وَخَالَفْنَاهُمْ، لِمَا سَبَقَ إِلَيْنَا مِنَ الشَقْوة الَّتِي كُنَّا نَسْتَحِقُّهَا حَيْثُ عَدَلْنا عَنِ الْحَقِّ إِلَى الْبَاطِلِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْهُمْ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿كُلَّمَا أُلْقِيَ فِيهَا فَوْجٌ سَأَلَهُمْ خَزَنَتُهَا أَلَمْ يَأْتِكُمْ نَذِيرٌ قَالُوا بَلَى قَدْ جَاءَنَا نَذِيرٌ فَكَذَّبْنَا وَقُلْنَا مَا نزلَ اللَّهُ مِنْ شَيْءٍ إِنْ أَنْتُمْ إِلا فِي ضَلالٍ كَبِيرٍ وَقَالُوا لَوْ كُنَّا نَسْمَعُ أَوْ نَعْقِلُ مَا كُنَّا فِي أَصْحَابِ السَّعِيرِ﴾ [الْمُلْكِ:٨-١٠] ، أَيْ: رَجَعُوا عَلَى أَنْفُسِهِمْ بِالْمَلَامَةِ وَالنَّدَامَةِ ﴿فَاعْتَرَفُوا بِذَنْبِهِمْ فَسُحْقًا لأصْحَابِ السَّعِيرِ﴾ [الْمُلْكِ:١١] أَيْ: بُعْدًا لَهُمْ وَخَسَارًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ هَاهُنَا: ﴿قِيلَ ادْخُلُوا أَبْوَابَ جَهَنَّمَ خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا﴾ أَيْ: كُلُّ مَنْ رَآهُمْ وَعَلِمَ حَالَهُمْ يَشْهَدُ عَلَيْهِمْ بِأَنَّهُمْ مُسْتَحِقُّونَ لِلْعَذَابِ؛ وَلِهَذَا لَمْ يُسْنِدْ هَذَا الْقَوْلَ إِلَى قَائِلٍ مُعَيَّنٍ، بَلْ أَطْلَقَهُ لِيَدُلَّ عَلَى أَنَّ الْكَوْنَ شَاهِدٌ عَلَيْهِمْ بِأَنَّهُمْ مُسْتَحِقُّونَ مَا هُمْ فِيهِ بِمَا حَكَمَ الْعَدْلُ الْخَبِيرُ عَلَيْهِمْ بِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ جَلَّ وَعَلَا ﴿قِيلَ ادْخُلُوا أَبْوَابَ جَهَنَّمَ خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا﴾ أَيْ: مَاكِثِينَ فِيهَا لَا خُرُوجَ لَكُمْ مِنْهَا، وَلَا زَوَالَ لَكُمْ عَنْهَا، ﴿فَبِئْسَ مَثْوَى الْمُتَكَبِّرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: فَبِئْسَ الْمَصِيرُ وَبِئْسَ الْمَقِيلُ لَكُمْ، بِسَبَبِ تَكَبُّرِكُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا، وَإِبَائِكُمْ عَنِ اتِّبَاعِ الْحَقِّ، فَهُوَ الَّذِي صَيَّرَكُمْ إِلَى مَا أَنْتُمْ فِيهِ، فَبِئْسَ الْحَالُ وَبِئْسَ الْمَآلُ.

---

## 39:73-74 — verses 73-74 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is a report about the state of the fortunate believers when they are driven upon swift mounts as a delegation to Paradise. {In companies}, that is, group after group: the ones brought near, then the righteous ones, then those who follow them, then those who follow after them, each party together with those most fitting to it: the prophets with the prophets, the truthful ones (siddiqun) with those resembling them, the martyrs with their counterparts, the scholars with their peers, each category with its category, each company suited to one another.

{Until, when they reach it}, that is, they arrive at the gates of Paradise after crossing the Sirat (the bridge), they are held back upon a bridge between Paradise and the Fire, and the wrongs that occurred among them in the worldly life are settled in retribution between them, until, when they have been purified and cleansed, they are permitted to enter Paradise. It has been reported in the hadith of the Trumpet that the believers, when they arrive at the gates of Paradise, will consult among themselves as to who should seek permission for them to enter, and they will go to Adam, then Noah, then Abraham, then Moses, then Jesus, then Muhammad, may the prayers and peace of Allah be upon them all, just as they did in the open plains (al-'arasat) when they sought intercession to Allah, mighty and majestic, that He come to render judgment, so that the nobility of Muhammad ﷺ would become manifest above the rest of mankind in every station.

It is established in Sahih Muslim on the authority of Anas, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "I am the first intercessor in Paradise." And in another wording of Muslim's: "And I am the first to knock upon the gate of Paradise."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Anas ibn Malik, may Allah be pleased with him, said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "I will come to the gate of Paradise on the Day of Resurrection and ask that it be opened. The keeper will say: Who are you? I will say: Muhammad. He said, the keeper will say: I was commanded because of you not to open for anyone before you."

Muslim narrated it as well, [chain] from Thabit, from Anas, with the same content.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "The first company to enter Paradise will have faces like the moon on the night it is full. They will not spit in it, nor blow their noses in it, nor relieve themselves in it. Their vessels and their combs will be of gold and silver, their censers will burn aloeswood, and their sweat will be musk. Each one of them will have two wives, so beautiful that the marrow of their shins will be visible through the flesh. There will be no disagreement or mutual hatred among them; their hearts will be as one heart, glorifying Allah morning and evening."

Al-Bukhari narrated it [chain] from Ibn al-Mubarak. Muslim narrated it [chain] from 'Abd al-Razzaq, both from Ma'mar with his chain, in similar wording. It was likewise narrated by Abu al-Zinad, from al-A'raj, from Abu Hurayrah [may Allah be pleased with him], from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ.

The hafiz Abu Ya'la said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah [may Allah be pleased with him] said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "The first company to enter Paradise will be like the moon on the night it is full, and those who follow them will be like the brightest star in the sky in radiance. They will not urinate, nor relieve themselves, nor spit, nor blow their noses. Their combs will be of gold, their sweat will be musk, their censers will burn aloeswood, and their spouses will be the wide-eyed maidens (al-hur al-'in). Their character will all be as the character of a single man, upon the form of their father Adam, sixty cubits tall in the sky."

Both [al-Bukhari and Muslim] also extracted it through the hadith of Jarir.

Al-Zuhri said, from Sa'id, from Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, who said: "A company of my nation will enter Paradise, seventy thousand of them, their faces shining like the moon on the night it is full." 'Ukkashah ibn Mihsan stood and said: O Messenger of Allah, pray to Allah that He make me one of them. He said, "O Allah, make him one of them." Then a man from the Ansar stood and said: O Messenger of Allah, pray to Allah that He make me one of them. The Prophet ﷺ said, "'Ukkashah has preceded you in that."

Both [al-Bukhari and Muslim] extracted it. This hadith, concerning the seventy thousand who will enter Paradise without reckoning, was also narrated by al-Bukhari and Muslim from Ibn 'Abbas, Jabir ibn 'Abd Allah, 'Imran ibn Husayn, Ibn Mas'ud, Rifa'ah ibn 'Arabah al-Juhani, and Umm Qays bint Mihsan.

Both of them [al-Bukhari and Muslim] also have, from Abu Hazim, from Sahl ibn Sa'd, that the Messenger of Allah, may Allah's peace and blessings be upon him, said: "Seventy thousand of my nation, or seven hundred thousand, will certainly enter Paradise holding onto one another, so that the first of them and the last of them will enter Paradise together, their faces like the moon on the night it is full."

Abu Bakr ibn Abi Shaybah said: [chain] I heard Abu Umamah al-Bahili say: I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say, "My Lord, mighty and majestic, has promised me that He will admit into Paradise from my nation seventy thousand, with every thousand another seventy thousand, with no reckoning and no punishment upon them, and three handfuls from the handfuls of my Lord, mighty and majestic."

It was likewise narrated by al-Walid ibn Muslim, from Safwan ibn 'Amr, from Sulaym ibn 'Amir [and] Abu al-Yaman 'Amir ibn 'Abd Allah ibn Luhayy, from Abu Umamah [may Allah be pleased with him].

Al-Tabarani narrated it, from 'Utbah ibn 'Abd al-Sulami: "Then every thousand will be granted intercession for seventy thousand."

The like of it has been narrated from Thawban and Abu Sa'id al-Anmari, and it has supporting reports (shawahid) from many avenues.

As for His saying: {Until, when they reach it, and its gates are opened, and its keepers say to them, "Peace be upon you, you have been good and pure, so enter it, abiding therein forever"}, the response (of the conditional clause) is not mentioned here. Its implied meaning is: until, when they reach it, and these matters occur, namely the opening of the gates for them as an honor and a glorification, and the angelic keepers receive them with glad tidings, greetings of peace, and praise, unlike how the guardian angels (al-zabaniyah) receive the disbelievers with rebuke and reproach, the implied response is: when this happens, they will be happy and pure, delighted and joyful, according to whatever bliss will be theirs therein. When the response is omitted here, the mind wanders in every direction of hope and expectation.

Whoever claims that the "wa" (and) in His saying {and its gates are opened} is the "wa of eight" (waw al-thamaniyah), and uses it as evidence that the gates of Paradise are eight, has gone far in his search and overreached in his effort. The fact that the gates of Paradise are eight is established only from the authentic hadiths.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "Whoever spends a pair of something from his wealth in the way of Allah will be called from the gates of Paradise, and Paradise has gates: whoever was among the people of prayer will be called from the gate of prayer, whoever was among the people of charity will be called from the gate of charity, whoever was among the people of jihad will be called from the gate of jihad, and whoever was among the people of fasting will be called from the gate of al-Rayyan." Abu Bakr, may Allah be pleased with him, said: O Messenger of Allah, there is no necessity upon anyone as to which gate he is called from, whichever it is he is called from; but will anyone be called from all of them, O Messenger of Allah? He said, "Yes, and I hope that you will be among them."

Al-Bukhari and Muslim narrated it from the hadith of al-Zuhri, in similar wording.

Both of them also have, from the hadith of Abu Hazim Salamah ibn Dinar, from Sahl ibn Sa'd, that the Messenger of Allah, may Allah's peace and blessings be upon him, said: "In Paradise there are eight gates; one of them is called al-Rayyan, which none enters except those who fasted."

In Sahih Muslim, from 'Umar ibn al-Khattab, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "There is not one of you who performs ablution, and does so thoroughly, or perfects the ablution, then says: I bear witness that there is no god but Allah, and that Muhammad is His servant and messenger, except that the eight gates of Paradise are opened for him, and he may enter from whichever of them he wishes."

Al-Hasan ibn 'Arafah said: [chain] Mu'adh, may Allah be pleased with him, said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "The key to Paradise is: there is no god but Allah."

Mention of the vastness of the gates of Paradise, we ask Allah the Immense, out of His bounty, to make us among its people:

In the two Sahihs, from the hadith of Abu Zur'ah, from Abu Hurayrah [may Allah be pleased with him], in the lengthy hadith of intercession: "Allah will say: O Muhammad, admit whoever has no reckoning upon him..."

from among your nation through the right-hand gate, and they share with the rest of the people the other gates. By the One in whose hand is the soul of Muhammad, what is between the two panels of one of the doors of Paradise, between the two doorposts of the gate, is like the distance between Mecca and Hajar, or Hajar and Mecca." In another narration: "Mecca and Busra."

In Sahih Muslim, from Utbah ibn Ghazwan, that he delivered a sermon to them in which he said: "It has indeed been mentioned to us that what is between two panels of the doors of Paradise is a journey of forty years, and there will surely come upon it a day when it will be packed tight from the crowding."

In the Musnad, from Hakim ibn Muawiyah, from his father, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, the like of it.

Abd ibn Humayd said: [chain] Abu Sa'id, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, who said: "What is between two panels of Paradise is a journey of forty years."

His saying: {And its keepers will say to them, 'Peace be upon you, you have been good'} that is, your deeds were good and your words were good, and your striving was good, so your reward was good, just as the Messenger of Allah ﷺ commanded it to be proclaimed among the Muslims during one of the campaigns: "No one enters Paradise except a soul that is Muslim." In another narration: "believing."

His saying: {So enter it, abiding therein forever} that is, remaining in it forever, never desiring to be transferred away from it.

{And they will say, 'Praise be to Allah who has fulfilled His promise to us'} that is, the believers say, when they behold in Paradise that abundant reward, that great gift, that lasting bliss, that vast dominion, they say at that: {Praise be to Allah who has fulfilled His promise to us} that is, what He had promised us through the tongues of His noble messengers, just as they had prayed in the worldly life: {Our Lord, grant us what You have promised us through Your messengers, and do not disgrace us on the Day of Resurrection. Indeed, You do not break the promise} [Al Imran: 194], {And they will say, 'Praise be to Allah who has guided us to this, and we would not have been guided had Allah not guided us. Certainly the messengers of our Lord came with the truth'} [Al-A'raf: 43], {And they will say, 'Praise be to Allah who has removed grief from us. Indeed our Lord is Forgiving, Appreciative, He who has settled us in the home of permanent stay out of His bounty. No fatigue touches us therein, nor does any weariness touch us therein'} [Fatir: 34-35].

Their saying: {And He has made us inherit the land, settling wherever we wish in Paradise. How excellent is the reward of the workers} Abu al-Aliyah, Abu Salih, Qatadah, al-Suddi, and Ibn Zayd said: that is, the land of Paradise.

This verse is like His saying: {And We have already written in the Zabur, after the Reminder, that the earth will be inherited by My righteous servants} [Al-Anbiya: 105]. That is why they said: {settling wherever we wish in Paradise} that is, wherever we wish, we shall dwell, and how excellent is the reward, our reward for our deeds.

In the two Sahihs, from the hadith of al-Zuhri, from Anas, in the account of the Mi'raj, the Prophet ﷺ said: "I was brought into Paradise, and there were domes of pearl in it, and its soil was musk."

Abd ibn Humayd said: [chain] from Abu Sa'id (may Allah be pleased with him), that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ asked Ibn Sayyad about the soil of Paradise. He said: "White fine flour, pure musk." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "He has spoken the truth."

Muslim likewise narrated it from the hadith of Abu Maslamah, from Abu Nadrah, from Abu Sa'id, with it.

Muslim also narrated it from Abu Bakr ibn Abi Shaybah, from Abu Usamah, from al-Jurayri, from Abu Nadrah, from Abu Sa'id, that Ibn Sayyad asked the Messenger of Allah ﷺ about the soil of Paradise, and he said: "White fine flour, pure musk."

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from Ali ibn Abi Talib (may Allah be pleased with him), concerning His saying, the Exalted: {And those who feared their Lord will be driven to Paradise in groups}, he said: They will be driven until they reach one of the gates of Paradise, and they will find there a tree from beneath whose trunk two springs flow. They will proceed to one of them and purify themselves from it, and the freshness of bliss will flow over them, so that their skin will never change after that, ever, and their hair will never become disheveled after that, ever, as though they had been anointed with oil. Then they will proceed to the other spring, as though they had been commanded to do so, and they will drink from it, and it will remove whatever was in their bellies of impurity or filth. And the angels will meet them at the gates of Paradise: {Peace be upon you, you have been good, so enter it abiding forever}. Each group of young attendants will meet its companion, circling around him, the way young men do with someone dear who has returned from being away: "Rejoice, Allah has prepared for you such and such of honor, Allah has prepared for you such and such of honor." He said: And an attendant from among his young attendants will go to his wives among the wide-eyed houris and say: "This is so-and-so," by his worldly name, and they will say: "Have you seen him?" He will say: "Yes." Joy will make them so light with excitement that one of them will go out to the threshold of the door. He said: Then he comes, and there before him are cushions arranged in rows, and cups set out, and carpets spread about. He said: Then he looks at the foundation of his building, and he finds it founded upon rock of pearl, alternating red, green, yellow, and white, and of every color. Then he raises his gaze to its ceiling, and were it not that Allah had made it bearable for him, it would nearly take away his sight, for it is like lightning. Then he looks at his wives among the wide-eyed houris, then he reclines upon one of his couches, then he says: {Praise be to Allah who has guided us to this, and we would not have been guided had Allah not guided us} [Al-A'raf: 43], the verse.

Then he said: [chain] I heard Abu Mu'adh al-Basri say: Ali (may Allah be pleased with him) was one day with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and the Prophet ﷺ said: "By the One in whose hand is my soul, when they come out of their graves they will be received, or brought, camels with wings, upon which are saddles of gold, the straps of their sandals gleaming with light, each step of which spans as far as the eye can see. They will arrive at a tree from whose root two springs gush forth. They will drink from one of them, and whatever impurity was in their bellies will be washed away, and they will wash themselves from the other, so that their skin and their hair will never become disheveled after that, ever, and the freshness of bliss will flow over them. They will arrive, or come, to the gate of Paradise, and there will be a ring of red ruby upon plates of gold. They will strike the ring against the plate, and a ringing sound will be heard from it, O Ali, and it will reach every houri that her husband has arrived. She will send her keeper, who will open for him. When he sees him, he will fall down before him, Maslamah said: I think he said, prostrating, and he will say: 'Raise your head, for I am only your keeper, entrusted with your affair.' So he follows him and traces his steps, and eagerness overtakes the houri, so that she comes out from tents of pearl and ruby until she embraces him, then she says: 'You are my beloved, and I am your beloved, and I am the eternal one who never dies, and I am the one in bliss who never suffers hardship, and I am the pleased one who is never angered, and I am the abiding one who never departs.' Then he enters a dwelling whose foundation to its ceiling is a hundred thousand cubits, built upon rock of pearl, in bands of yellow, green, and red, no band resembling the one beside it. In the dwelling are seventy couches, on each couch seventy cushions, on each cushion seventy wives, on each wife seventy garments, the marrow of her leg visible through the garments. He will spend with her a period equal to one of your nights here. Rivers flow beneath them, rivers of water unaltered, he said: pure, with no murkiness in it, and rivers of milk whose taste never changes, he said: it did not come out of the udders of livestock, and rivers of wine delightful to those who drink, he said: it was not pressed by men with their feet, and rivers of purified honey, he said: it did not come from the bellies of bees. He gathers the fruit, if he wishes standing, if he wishes sitting, if he wishes reclining, then he recited: {And their shades will be close upon them, and their fruits made easy to reach} [Al-Insan: 14]. He desires food, and a white bird comes to him, he said: and sometimes he said green, it lowers its wings, and he eats from its sides whatever kind he wishes, then it flies away and departs. Then the angel enters and says: 'Peace be upon you. This is the Paradise you have inherited for what you used to do.' And if a single hair from the hair of the houri fell to the people of the earth, the sun would appear dim in darkness compared to its light."

This is a gharib (singular) hadith, and it appears to be mursal (a report in which the narrator omits the Companion and attributes it directly to the Prophet ﷺ). And Allah knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

وَهَذَا إِخْبَارٌ عَنْ حَالِ السُّعَدَاءِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ حِينَ يُسَاقُونَ عَلَى النَّجَائِبِ وَفْدًا إِلَى الْجَنَّةِ ﴿زُمَرًا﴾ أَيْ: جَمَاعَةً بَعْدَ جَمَاعَةٍ: الْمُقَرَّبُونَ، ثُمَّ الْأَبْرَارُ، ثُمَّ الَّذِينَ يَلُونَهُمْ، ثُمَّ الَّذِينَ يَلُونَهُمْ كُلُّ طَائِفَةٍ مَعَ مَنْ يُنَاسِبُهُمْ: الْأَنْبِيَاءُ مَعَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ وَالصِّدِّيقُونَ مَعَ أَشْكَالِهِمْ، وَالشُّهَدَاءُ مَعَ أَضَرَابِهِمْ، وَالْعُلَمَاءُ مَعَ أَقْرَانِهِمْ، وَكُلُّ صِنْفٍ مَعَ صِنْفٍ، كُلُّ زُمْرَةٍ تُنَاسِبُ بَعْضُهَا بَعْضًا.

﴿حَتَّى إِذَا جَاءُوهَا﴾ أَيْ: وَصَلُوا إِلَى أَبْوَابِ الْجَنَّةِ بَعْدَ مُجَاوَزَةِ الصِّرَاطِ حُبِسُوا عَلَى قَنْطَرَةٍ بَيْنَ الْجَنَّةِ وَالنَّارِ، فَاقْتَصَّ لَهُمْ مَظَالِمُ كَانَتْ بَيْنَهُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا، حَتَّى إِذَا هُذِّبُوا ونُقُّوا أُذِنَ لَهُمْ فِي دُخُولِ الْجَنَّةِ، وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِي حَدِيثِ الصُّوَرِ أَنَّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ إِذَا انْتَهَوْا إِلَى أَبْوَابِ الْجَنَّةِ تَشَاوَرُوا فِيمَنْ يَسْتَأْذِنُ لَهُمْ بِالدُّخُولِ، فَيَقْصِدُونَ، آدَمَ، ثُمَّ نُوحًا، ثُمَّ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، ثُمَّ مُوسَى، ثُمَّ عِيسَى، ثُمَّ مُحَمَّدًا، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِمْ أَجْمَعِينَ، كَمَا فَعَلُوا فِي الْعَرَصَاتِ عِنْدَ اسْتِشْفَاعِهِمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، أَنْ يَأْتِيَ لِفَصْلِ الْقَضَاءِ، لِيَظْهَرَ شَرَفُ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ عَلَى سَائِرِ الْبَشَرِ فِي الْمَوَاطِنِ كُلِّهَا.

وَقَدْ ثَبَتَ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ عَنْ أَنَسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَنَا أَوَّلُ شَفِيعٍ فِي الْجَنَّةِ" وَفِي لَفْظٍ لِمُسْلِمٍ: "وَأَنَا أَوَّلُ مَنْ يَقْرَعُ بَابَ الْجَنَّةِ". .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا هَاشِمٌ، حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنْ ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "آتِي بَابَ الْجَنَّةِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ فَأَسْتَفْتِحُ، فَيَقُولُ الْخَازِنُ: مَنْ أَنْتَ؟ فَأَقُولُ: مُحَمَّدٌ. قَالَ: يَقُولُ: بِكَ أُمِرْتُ أَلَّا أَفْتَحَ لِأَحَدٍ قَبْلَكَ".

وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ عَنْ عَمْرٍو النَّاقِدِ وَزُهَيْرِ بْنِ حَرْبٍ، كِلَاهُمَا عَنْ أَبِي النَّضْرِ هَاشِمِ بْنِ الْقَاسِمِ، عَنْ سُلَيْمَانَ -وَهُوَ ابْنُ الْمُغِيرَةِ الْقَيْسِيُّ-عَنْ ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ، بِهِ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ حَدَّثَنَا مَعْمَر عَنْ هَمَّامِ بْنِ مُنَبِّهٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَوَّلُ زُمْرَةٍ تَلِجُ الْجَنَّةَ صُوَرُهُمْ عَلَى صُورَةِ الْقَمَرِ لَيْلَةَ الْبَدْرِ، لَا يَبْصُقُونَ فِيهَا، وَلَا يَمْتَخِطُونَ فِيهَا، وَلَا يَتَغَوَّطُونَ فِيهَا. آنِيَتُهُمْ وَأَمْشَاطُهُمُ الذَّهَبُ وَالْفِضَّةُ، وَمُجَامِرُهُمُ الْأَلُوَّةُ ، ورَشْحُهُمُ الْمِسْكُ، وَلِكُلِّ وَاحِدٍ مِنْهُمْ زَوْجَتَانِ، يَرَى مُخَّ سَاقِهِمَا مِنْ وَرَاءِ اللَّحْمِ مِنَ الْحُسْنِ. لَا اخْتِلَافَ بَيْنِهِمْ وَلَا تَبَاغُضَ، قُلُوبُهُمْ عَلَى قَلْبٍ وَاحِدٍ يُسَبِّحُونَ اللَّهَ بُكْرَةً وَعَشِيًّا".

رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ مُقَاتِلٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ الْمُبَارَكِ. وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ رَافِعٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّزَّاقِ، كِلَاهُمَا عَنْ مَعْمَرٍ بِإِسْنَادِهِ نَحْوَهُ . وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ أَبُو الزِّنَادِ، عَنِ الْأَعْرَجِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ .

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو يَعْلَى: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو خَيْثَمة، حَدَّثَنَا جَرِيرٌ، عَنْ عُمَارَةَ بْنِ الْقَعْقَاعِ، عَنْ أَبِي زُرْعَة، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أول زُمْرَة يَدْخُلُونَ الْجَنَّةَ عَلَى صُورَةِ الْقَمَرِ لَيْلَةَ الْبَدْرِ، وَالَّذِينَ يَلُونَهُمْ عَلَى ضَوْءِ أشدُّ كَوْكَبٍ دُرِّي فِي السَّمَاءِ إِضَاءَةً، لَا يَبُولُونَ وَلَا يَتَغَوَّطُونَ وَلَا يتْفلون وَلَا يَمْتَخِطُونَ، أَمْشَاطُهُمُ الذَّهَبُ وَرَشْحُهُمُ الْمِسْكُ، وَمَجَامِرُهُمُ الْأَلُوَّةُ، وَأَزْوَاجُهُمُ الْحُورُ الْعِينُ، أخلاقهم على خلق رجل واحد، على صورة أَبِيهِمْ آدَمَ، سِتُّونَ ذِرَاعًا فِي السَّمَاءِ" .

وَأَخْرَجَاهُ أَيْضًا مِنْ حَدِيثِ جَرِيرٍ .

وَقَالَ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ سَعِيدٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "يَدْخُلُ الْجَنَّةَ مِنْ أُمَّتِي زُمْرَة، هُمْ سَبْعُونَ أَلْفًا، تُضِيءُ وُجُوهُهُمْ إِضَاءَةَ الْقَمَرِ لَيْلَةَ الْبَدْرِ". فَقَامَ عُكَّاشة بْنُ مِحْصَن فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ادْعُ اللَّهَ، أَنْ يَجْعَلَنِي مِنْهُمْ: فَقَالَ: "اللَّهُمَّ اجْعَلْهُ مِنْهُمْ". ثُمَّ قَامَ رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، ادْعُ اللَّهَ أَنْ يَجْعَلَنِي مِنْهُمْ. فَقَالَ ﷺ: "سَبَقَكَ بِهَا عُكَّاشة".

أَخْرَجَاهُ وَقَدْ رَوَى هَذَا الْحَدِيثَ -فِي السَّبْعِينَ أَلْفًا يَدْخُلُونَ الْجَنَّةَ بِغَيْرِ حِسَابٍ-الْبُخَارِيُّ وَمُسْلِمٌ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَجَابِرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، وَعِمْرَانَ بْنِ حصين، وابن مسعود، ورفاعة بن عرابة الْجُهَنِيِّ، وَأُمِّ قَيْسٍ بِنْتِ مِحْصَنٍ.

وَلَهُمَا عَنْ أَبِي حَازِمٍ، عَنْ سَهْلِ بْنِ سَعْدٍ، أَنَّ رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم قال: "لَيَدْخُلَنَّ الْجَنَّةَ مِنْ أُمَّتِي سَبْعُونَ أَلْفًا -أَوْ: سَبْعُمِائَةِ أَلْفٍ-آخذٌ بَعْضُهُمْ بِبَعْضٍ، حَتَّى يَدْخُلَ أَوَّلُهُمْ وَآخِرُهُمُ الْجَنَّةَ، وُجُوهُهُمْ عَلَى صُورَةِ الْقَمَرِ لَيْلَةَ الْبَدْرِ". .

وَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ عَيَّاشٍ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ زِيَادٍ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ أَبَا أُمَامَةَ الْبَاهِلِيَّ يَقُولُ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: وَعَدَنِي رَبِّي، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، أَنْ يُدْخِلَ الْجَنَّةَ مِنْ أُمَّتِي سَبْعُونَ أَلْفًا، مَعَ كُلِّ أَلْفٍ سَبْعُونَ أَلْفًا، وَلَا حِسَابَ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا عَذَابَ، وَثَلَاثُ حَثَيَات مِنْ حَثَيَاتِ رَبِّي عَزَّ وَجَلَّ" .

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ الْوَلِيدُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ صَفْوَانُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو، عَنْ سُلَيْمِ بْنِ عَامِرٍ [وَ] أَبِي الْيَمَانِ عَامِرُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ لحُيّ عَنْ أَبِي أُمَامَةَ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] .

وَرَوَاهُ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ، عَنْ عُتْبَةَ بْنِ عَبْدٍ السُّلمي: "ثُمَّ يُشَفَّعُ كُلُّ أَلْفٍ فِي سَبْعِينَ أَلْفًا" .

وَرُوِيَ مِثْلُهُ، عَنْ ثَوْبَانَ وَأَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْأَنْمَارِيِّ، وَلَهُ شَوَاهِدُ مِنْ وُجُوهٍ كَثِيرَةٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا جَاءُوهَا وَفُتِحَتْ أَبْوَابُهَا وَقَالَ لَهُمْ خَزَنَتُهَا سَلامٌ عَلَيْكُمْ طِبْتُمْ فَادْخُلُوهَا خَالِدِينَ﴾ لَمْ يَذْكُرِ الْجَوَابَ هَاهُنَا، وَتَقْدِيرُهُ: حَتَّى إِذَا جَاءُوهَا، وَكَانَتْ هَذِهِ الْأُمُورُ مِنْ فَتْحِ الْأَبْوَابِ لَهُمْ إِكْرَامًا وَتَعْظِيمًا، وَتَلَقَّتْهُمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ الْخَزَنَةُ بِالْبِشَارَةِ وَالسَّلَامِ وَالثَّنَاءِ، لَا كَمَا تَلْقَى الزَّبَانِيَةُ الْكَفَرَةَ بِالتَّثْرِيبِ وَالتَّأْنِيبِ، فَتَقْدِيرُهُ: إِذَا كَانَ هَذَا سَعِدوا وَطَابُوا، وسُرّوا وَفَرِحُوا، بِقَدْرِ كُلِّ مَا يَكُونُ لَهُمْ فِيهِ نَعِيمٌ. وَإِذَا حُذِفَ الْجَوَابُ هَاهُنَا ذَهَبَ الذِّهْنُ كُلَّ مَذْهَبٍ فِي الرَّجَاءِ وَالْأَمَلِ.

وَمَنْ زَعَمَ أَنَّ "الْوَاوَ" فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَفُتِحَتْ أَبْوَابُهَا﴾ وَاوُ الثَّمَانِيَةِ، وَاسْتُدِلَّ بِهِ عَلَى أَنَّ أَبْوَابَ الْجَنَّةِ ثَمَانِيَةٌ، فَقَدْ أَبْعَدَ النّجْعَة وَأَغْرَقَ فِي النَّزْعِ. وَإِنَّمَا يُسْتَفَادُ كَوْنُ أَبْوَابِ الْجَنَّةِ ثَمَانِيَةٌ مِنَ الْأَحَادِيثِ الصَّحِيحَةِ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَخْبَرَنَا مَعْمَرٌ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ عَنْ حُمَيْدِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَنْ أَنْفَقَ زَوْجَيْنِ مِنْ مَالِهِ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، دُعِيَ مِنْ أَبْوَابِ الْجَنَّةِ، وَلِلْجَنَّةِ أَبْوَابٌ ، فَمَنْ كَانَ مَنْ أَهْلِ الصَّلَاةِ دُعِي مِنْ بَابِ الصَّلَاةِ، وَمَنْ كَانَ مَنْ أَهْلِ الصَّدَقَةِ دُعِيَ مِنْ بَابِ الصَّدَقَةِ، وَمَنْ كَانَ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْجِهَادِ دُعِيَ مِنْ بَابِ الْجِهَادِ، وَمَنْ كَانَ مِنْ أَهْلِ الصِّيَامِ دُعِيَ مِنْ بَابِ الرَّيَّانِ" فَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى عَنْهُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، مَا عَلَى أَحَدٍ مِنْ ضَرُورَةٍ دُعي، مِنْ أَيِّهَا دُعِيَ، فَهَلْ يُدْعَى مِنْهَا كُلِّهَا أَحَدٌ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "نَعَمْ، وَأَرْجُو أَنْ تَكُونَ مِنْهُمْ".

وَرَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ وَمُسْلِمٌ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، بِنَحْوِهِ .

وَفِيهِمَا مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي حَازِمٍ سَلَمَةَ بْنِ دِينَارٍ ، عَنْ سَهْلِ بْنِ سَعْدٍ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم قال: "إِنَّ فِي الْجَنَّةِ ثَمَانِيَةَ أَبْوَابٍ، بَابٌ مِنْهَا يُسَمَّى الرَّيَّانُ، لَا يَدْخُلُهُ إِلَّا الصَّائِمُونَ" .

وَفِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا مِنْكُمْ مِنْ أَحَدٍ يَتَوَضَّأُ فَيُبْلِغَ -أَوْ: فَيُسْبِغَ الْوُضُوءَ-ثُمَّ يَقُولُ: أَشْهَدُ أَنْ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، وَأَنَّ مُحَمَّدًا عَبْدُهُ وَرَسُولُهُ، إِلَّا فُتِحَتْ لَهُ أَبْوَابُ الْجَنَّةِ الثَّمَانِيَةُ، يَدْخُلُ مِنْ أَيِّهَا شَاءَ". .

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ بْنُ عَرَفَةَ: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ عَيَّاشٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ أَبِي حُسَين، عَنْ شَهْر بْنِ حَوْشَب، عَنْ مُعَاذٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مِفْتَاحُ الْجَنَّةِ: لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ" .

ذِكْرُ سَعَةِ أَبْوَابِ الْجَنَّةِ -نَسْأَلُ اللَّهَ الْعَظِيمَ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ أَنْ يَجْعَلَنَا مِنْ أَهْلِهَا-:

فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ حَدِيثَ أَبِي زُرْعَة، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] فِي حَدِيثِ الشَّفَاعَةِ الطَّوِيلِ: "فَيَقُولُ اللَّهُ يَا مُحَمَّدُ، أَدْخِلْ مَنْ لَا حِسَابَ عَلَيْهِ .

مِنْ أُمَّتِكَ مِنَ الْبَابِ الْأَيْمَنِ، وَهُمْ شُرَكَاءُ النَّاسِ فِي الْأَبْوَابِ الْأُخَرِ. وَالَّذِي نَفْسُ مُحَمَّدٍ بِيَدِهِ، إِنَّ مَا بَيْنَ الْمِصْرَاعَيْنِ مِنْ مَصَارِيعِ الْجَنَّةِ -مَا بَيْنَ عِضَادَتَيِ الْبَابِ-لَكُمَا بَيْنَ مَكَّةَ وَهَجَرٍ-أَوْ هَجَرٍ وَمَكَّةَ". وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: "مَكَّةَ وَبُصْرَى" .

وَفِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ عُتْبَةَ بْنِ غَزْوَانَ أَنَّهُ خَطَبَهُمْ خُطْبَةً فَقَالَ فِيهَا: "وَلَقَدْ ذُكِرَ لَنَا أَنَّ مَا بَيْنَ مِصْرَاعَيْنِ مِنْ مَصَارِيعِ الْجَنَّةِ، مَسِيرَةُ أَرْبَعِينَ سَنَةً، وَلِيَأْتِيَنَّ عَلَيْهِ يَوْمٌ وَهُوَ كَظِيظٌ مِنَ الزِّحَامِ" .

وَفِي الْمُسْنَدِ عَنْ حَكِيمِ بْنِ مُعَاوِيَةَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، مِثْلُهُ .

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ بْنُ حُمَيْدٍ: حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ مُوسَى، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ لَهِيعَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا دَرَّاج، عَنْ أَبِي الْهَيْثَمِ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قال: "إِنَّ مَا بَيْنَ مِصْرَاعَيْنِ فِي الْجَنَّةِ مَسِيرَةُ أَرْبَعِينَ سَنَةً" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَقَالَ لَهُمْ خَزَنَتُهَا سَلامٌ عَلَيْكُمْ طِبْتُمْ﴾ أَيْ: طَابَتْ أَعْمَالُكُمْ وَأَقْوَالُكُمْ، وَطَابَ سَعْيُكُمْ فَطَابَ جَزَاؤُكُمْ، كَمَا أَمْرَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنْ يُنَادَى بَيْنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ فِي بَعْضِ الْغَزَوَاتِ: "إِنَّ الْجَنَّةَ لَا يَدْخُلُهَا إِلَّا نَفْسٌ مُسْلِمَةٌ" وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: "مُؤْمِنَةٌ". .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَادْخُلُوهَا خَالِدِينَ﴾ أَيْ: مَاكِثِينَ فِيهَا أَبَدًا، لَا يَبْغُونَ عَنْهَا حِوَلًا.

﴿وَقَالُوا الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي صَدَقَنَا وَعْدَهُ﴾ أَيْ: يَقُولُ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ إِذَا عَايَنُوا فِي الْجَنَّةِ ذَلِكَ الثَّوَابَ الْوَافِرَ، وَالْعَطَاءَ الْعَظِيمَ، وَالنَّعِيمَ الْمُقِيمَ، وَالْمُلْكَ الْكَبِيرَ، يَقُولُونَ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ: ﴿الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي صَدَقَنَا وَعْدَهُ﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِي كَانَ وَعَدَنَا عَلَى أَلْسِنَةِ رُسُلِهِ الْكِرَامِ، كَمَا دَعَوْا فِي الدُّنْيَا: ﴿رَبَّنَا وَآتِنَا مَا وَعَدْتَنَا عَلَى رُسُلِكَ وَلا تُخْزِنَا يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ إِنَّكَ لَا تُخْلِفُ الْمِيعَادَ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ: ١٩٤] ، ﴿وَقَالُوا الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي هَدَانَا لِهَذَا وَمَا كُنَّا لِنَهْتَدِيَ لَوْلا أَنْ هَدَانَا اللَّهُ لَقَدْ جَاءَتْ رُسُلُ رَبِّنَا بِالْحَقِّ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ:٤٣] ، ﴿وَقَالُوا الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي أَذْهَبَ عَنَّا الْحَزَنَ إِنَّ رَبَّنَا لَغَفُورٌ شَكُورٌ الَّذِي أَحَلَّنَا دَارَ الْمُقَامَةِ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ لَا يَمَسُّنَا فِيهَا نَصَبٌ وَلا يَمَسُّنَا فِيهَا لُغُوبٌ﴾ [فَاطِرٍ:٣٥، ٣٤] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُمْ: ﴿وَأَوْرَثَنَا الأرْضَ نَتَبَوَّأُ مِنَ الْجَنَّةِ حَيْثُ نَشَاءُ فَنِعْمَ أَجْرُ الْعَامِلِينَ﴾ قَالَ أَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ، وَأَبُو صَالِحٍ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَابْنُ زَيْدٍ : أَيْ أَرْضِ الْجَنَّةِ.

وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ كَتَبْنَا فِي الزَّبُورِ مِنْ بَعْدِ الذِّكْرِ أَنَّ الأرْضَ يَرِثُهَا عِبَادِيَ الصَّالِحُونَ﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ:١٠٥] ، وَلِهَذَا قَالُوا: ﴿نَتَبَوَّأُ مِنَ الْجَنَّةِ حَيْثُ نَشَاءُ﴾ أَيْ: أَيْنَ شِئْنَا حَلَلْنَا، فَنِعْمَ الْأَجْرُ أَجْرُنَا عَلَى عَمَلِنَا.

وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ فِي قِصَّةِ الْمِعْرَاجِ قَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "أُدْخِلْتُ الْجَنَّةَ، فَإِذَا فِيهَا جَنَابِذُ اللُّؤْلُؤِ، وَإِذَا تُرَابُهَا الْمِسْكُ" .

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ بْنُ حُمَيْدٍ: حَدَّثَنَا رَوْحُ بْنُ عُبَادَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْجُرَيْرِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي نَضْرَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى الله عليه وسلم سَأَلَ ابْنَ صَائِدٍ عَنْ تُرْبَةِ الْجَنَّةِ؟ فَقَالَ: دَرْمَكة بيضاءُ مِسْك خَالِصٌ: فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "صَدَقَ".

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي مَسْلَمَةَ ، عَنْ أَبِي نَضْرَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ، بِهِ .

وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ [أَيْضًا] عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرِ بْنِ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي أُسَامَةَ، عَنِ الجُرَيْرِي، عَنْ أَبِي نَضْرَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ؛ أَنَّ ابْنَ صَائِدٍ سَأَلَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَنْ تُرْبَةِ الْجَنَّةِ، فَقَالَ: "دَرْمكة بَيْضَاءُ مِسْكٌ خَالِصٌ" .

وَقَوْلُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو غَسَّانَ مَالِكُ بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ عَاصِمِ بْنِ ضَمْرَةَ ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ أَبِي طَالِبٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَسِيقَ الَّذِينَ اتَّقَوْا رَبَّهُمْ إِلَى الْجَنَّةِ زُمَرًا﴾ ، قَالَ: سِيقُوا حَتَّى انْتَهَوْا إِلَى بَابٍ مِنْ أَبْوَابِ الْجَنَّةِ،
